## Idea

The sign of a permutation is defined as the parity of the length of the decomposition of the permutation into transpositions. We show that each such decomposition as the same parity, so the sign map is well defined. We then show that the sign map is a group homomorphism.

## Definitions

### The sign homomorphism into ℤ/2

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5860" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5867" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5867" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="5871" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5872" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5872" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5874" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5876" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5881" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5884" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5884" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="5886" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5888" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="5889" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5891" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5892" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5894" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5896" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5149" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="5909" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5872" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5911" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5884" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5912" class="Symbol">)</a> 
  <a id="5917" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5926" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5926" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="5952" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5954" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1297" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="5958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5959" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5244" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="5977" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5978" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5980" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5982" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2293" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="5986" class="Number">2</a>
  <a id="5990" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5926" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6016" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6016" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6018" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6024" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="6028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6029" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#1098" class="Function">center</a> <a id="6036" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6037" href="finite-group-theory.permutations.html#20688" class="Function">is-contr-parity-transposition-permutation</a> <a id="6079" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5884" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6081" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6083" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6016" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6084" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="6090" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6090" class="Function">preserves-add-sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6130" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6137" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6137" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6139" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6139" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="6141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6144" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5244" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6162" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6163" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6165" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="6167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6168" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5244" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6186" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6187" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6190" class="Symbol">→</a>

      <a id="6409" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6411" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5350" class="Function">has-cardinality-type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6445" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6446" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="6617" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6619" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6621" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6621" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6623" class="Symbol">→</a>
        <a id="6633" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6635" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>

                <a id="9336" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9338" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="9340" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9341" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5244" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="9359" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9360" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9362" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9365" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9365" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9367" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9369" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2583" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="9389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9390" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9284" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9392" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9365" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9393" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
    <a id="9403" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9087" class="Function">list-trans</a> <a id="9414" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9414" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="9417" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9417" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="9419" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="9427" href="finite-group-theory.permutations.html#17024" class="Function">list-transpositions-permutation-count</a> <a id="9465" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9466" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5244" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="9484" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5892" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9485" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9488" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="9493" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5884" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="9495" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9417" class="Bound">h</a><a id="9496" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9498" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9414" class="Bound">f&#39;</a>

      <a id="9570" href="univalent-combinatorics.lists.html#2156" class="Datatype">list</a>

            <a id="9643" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9645" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="9647" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9647" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9649" class="Symbol">→</a>

         <a id="9924" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9926" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#11010" class="Function">permutation-list-transpositions</a>

                <a id="10663" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10665" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9087" class="Function">list-trans</a> <a id="10676" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6359" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10678" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#10010" class="Bound">h</a><a id="10679" class="Symbol">))</a>

### The sign homomorphism into the symmetric group S₂

<pre class="Agda"><a id="10750" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10757" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#10757" class="Module">_</a>

## Deloopings of the sign homomorphism
